                {^{for suggestions ~markSelected=markSelected ~searchText=searchText}}
                    {{if suggestions.length}}
                        {{if type=='history'}}
                            <button class="autocomplete__clear-all j-clear-history-all" type="button">Очистить историю</button>
                        {{/if}}
                        <ul class="autocomplete__list autocomplete__list--{{:type}}">
                            {{for suggestions ~type=type}}
                            <li class="autocomplete__item j-suggest" data-link="class{merge: selected toggle='selected'}">
                                <p class="autocomplete__text">
                                    {{if ~type!='brand'}}
                                    <span class="autocomplete__icon{{if ~type=='history'}} autocomplete__icon--clock{{else ~type=='catalog'}} loupe{{/if}}"></span>
                                    {{/if}}
                                    <span class="autocomplete__phrase">{{: ~markSelected(name, ~searchText)}}</span>
                                    {{if ~type=='brand'}}
                                        <span class="autocomplete__text-decor">бренд</span>
                                    {{/if}}
                                </p>
                                {{if ~type=='history'}}
                                <button class="autocomplete__clear j-clear-history" type="button">удалить</button>
                                {{/if}}
                                {{if ~type=='brand'}}
                                    <img class="autocomplete__brand-logo" src="{{> ~brandLogoUrl(brandId)}}" width="67" height="28" alt="{{> name}}">
                                {{/if}}                      
                            </li>
                            {{/for}}
                        </ul>
                    {{/if}}
                {{/for}}
            </div>
        </div>
    {{/if}}
</script>

<div class="popup-confirm-age j-popup-confirm-age">
    <button class="popup__close j-confirm-age-close" type="button">Закрыть</button>
    <div class="popup__content">
        <h2 class="popup__header">Подтвердите свой возраст</h2>
        <p>Данный раздел предназначен только для посетителей, достигших возраста 18 лет!</p>
        <div class="popup__btn">
            <button type="button" class="popup__btn-main j-confirm" data-link="{on confirm}">Да, мне есть 18 лет</button>
            <button type="button" class="popup__btn-base j-confirm-age-close" data-link="{on decline}">Нет</button>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>
        <div id="fastSubscribeGiftIcon" style="display: none; position: fixed; left: 0px; z-index: 12;">
            <a onClick="return false;">
                <img src="//static.wbstatic.net/i/fastSubscribe.png" usemap="#giftCloseButton">
